        (0-8): 9 x FFNLayer(
          (linear1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=2048, bias=True)

      (query_embed): Embedding(100, 256)
      (level_embed): Embedding(3, 256)
      (input_proj): ModuleList(
        (0-2): 3 x Sequential()
      )

      (mask_embed): MLP(

          (0-2): 3 x Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        )
      )
    )
  )
